9b3('bum): dang / smon pa med pa la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ mngon par shes pa rnams la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub
9b4('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams la slob pa
9b5('bum): yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
9b6('bum): sems dpa' chen po ni/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la slob pa yin//
9b7('bum): rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ snying rje chen po la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sangs
10a1('bum): rgya sa la 'das pa cod rgyad ladzub pa pad/ sna nga sgyung chub pa byung chub sems dpa sems dpa ldan paH/ rgyun duzugs pa'i sa sul
10a2('bum): ba yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pa ni/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
10a3('bum): sems dang chen po ni/ phyi ma thong ba'i 'bras bu la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pa na/ dgra bcom pa nyid la slob pa yin/ rab
10a4('bum): de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ rang byang chub la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa
10a5('bum): nyid la rlob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems
10a6('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ bslab pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thob par 'gyur ba yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ bdud ngas
10a7('bum): bdud kyi ris kyi lha rnams kyis 'pham par mi nus pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob kyi rnams dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ myur du phyir mi ldog pa'i sa bathob pa yin/ rab 'byor
10b1('bum): ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ bdag gi pha de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul la spyod pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
10b2('bum): chen po ni/ mgon du 'gyur ba'i chos rnams la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ byams pa chen po la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar
10b3('bum): slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ snying rje chen po la slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yo
10b4('bum): su dag par bya ba'i phyir slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar
10b5('bum): slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ rnam pa bcu gnyis lan gsum du bskor ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i phyir slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub
10b6('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya'o zhes slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni//
10b7('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir slob pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ 'chi ba med pa'i sgo dbye bar bya'o zhes slob pa
11a1('bum): yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ 'dus ma byas kyi khams bstan par bya'o zhes slob pa yin te/ rab 'byor sems can dma' bas ni
11a2('bum): bslab pa rgya chen po 'di la bslab par mi nus so/ / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang bslab pa 'di la slob pa de ni/ sems can thams cad 'khor ba las gdon par 'dod pa ste/ rab
11a3('bum): 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sems can dmyal bar mi skye'o// byol song gi skye gnas su mi skye'o// gshin rje'i 'jig rten du mi skye'o// yul mtha' 'khob tu mi
11a4('bum): skye'o/ / yul gcong rong can du mi skye'o// phyag bdar ba dang gdol pa'i rigs su mi skye'o// zhar bar mi 'gyur ro// sgur por mi 'gyur ro// zha bor mi 'gyur ro// yan lag skyon can du mi 'gyur ro// 'on par mi 'gyur ro//
11a5('bum): lag pa med par mi 'gyur ro// rkang pa med par mi 'gyur ro// dbang po dang mi ldan par mi 'gyur te/ dbang po yongs su tshang zhing dbang po ma tshang bar mi 'gyur ro// srog gcod par mi 'gyur ro// ma byin
11a6('bum): par len par mi 'gyur ro/ / 'dod pas log par g.yem par mi 'gyur ro// rdzun du smra bar mi 'gyur ro// phra ma can du mi 'gyur ro// zhe gcod par smra bar mi 'gyur ro// tshig bkyal pa can du
11a7('bum): mi 'gyur ro/ / chags sems can du mi 'gyur ro// gnod sems can du mi 'gyur ro// log par lta bar mi 'gyur ro// 'tsho ba log pas 'tsho bar mi 'gyur ro// yang dag pa ma yin pa yongs
11b1('bum): su 'dzin par mi 'gyur ro/ / tshul khrims ngan pa can du mi 'gyur ro// tshul khrims ngan pa yongs su 'dzin par mi 'gyur ro// rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
11b2('bum): bo ni rtsa lha tshe ring po'i nang du mi skye'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa gang gis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lha tshe ring por mi skye ba'i thabs mkhas pa de lta bu de
11b3('bum): la yod de/ de'ang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di nyid las thabs mkhas pa bstan pa ste/ thabs mkhas pa de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
11b4('bum): sems dpa' chen po ni/ bsam gtan rnams la'ang snyoms par 'jug/ tshad med pa rnams la'ang snyoms par 'jug/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la'ang snyoms par 'jug pa
11b5('bum): ste/ bsam gtan dang / tshad med pa dang / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyi dbang gis kyang mi skye'o// rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
11b6('bum): chen po ni/ 'di lta ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi yid la bya ba'i dri ma yongs su dag pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi stobs yongs su dag par thob par 'gyur ro//
11b7('bum): gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa lags na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos gang gis rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa 'thob par 'gyur
12a1('bum): ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa de bzhin no// rab 'byor chos thams cad ni
12a2('bum): rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa ste/ rab 'byor de ltar chos thams cad yongs su dag la/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spod pa'i tshe/ sems
12a3('bum): zhum pa med cing 'gong ba med pa de ni/ rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyis ni chos nyid de mi shes mi mthong bas/ sems can de dag
12a4('bum): gi don du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/ brtson
12a5('bum): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod do/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/ nang stong pa nyid la spyod/ phyi stong pa nyid la spyod/ phyi nang
12a6('bum): stong pa nyid la spyod/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la spyod/ chen po stong pa nyid la spyod/ don dam pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid la spyod/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la spyod
12a7('bum): mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ thog mo dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyod/ chos thams cad stong pa
12b1('bum): nyid la spyod/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la spyod/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la spyod/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyod/ dngos po med pa'i
12b2('bum): ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyod/ dran pa nye bar gzhog pa bzhi la spyod/ yang dag par spong ba bzhi la spyod/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la spyod/ dbang po lnga la spyod/ stobs lnga
12b3('bum): la spyod/ byang chub kyi yan lag bdun la spyod/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la spyod/ baphags pa'i bden pa bzhi la spyod/ bsam gtan bzhi la spyod/ tshad med pa
12b4('bum): bzhi la spyod/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms por 'jug pa bzhi la spyod/ rnam par thar pa brgyad la spyod/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la spyod/ rnam par thar ba'i
12b5('bum): sgo stong po nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la spyod/ mngon par shes pa rnams la spyod/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la spyod/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams la spyod// de bzhin
12b6('bum): gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la spyod/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi la spyod/ so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la spyod/ snying rje chen po la spyod/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la
12b7('bum): spyod/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la spyod/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyod/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyod/ dgra bcom pa nyid la spyod/ rang byang chub la spyod/
13a1('bum): bya/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid la spyod/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la spyod de/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ chos thams cad
13a2('bum): kyi stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa nyid rab tu thob par 'gyur te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sar mi ltung ngo // rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sems can
13a3('bum): thams cad kyi sems dang / spyod pa dang / g.yo ba rnams kyi pha rol tu phyin par 'gyur ro// rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper nas chen po'i phyogs gang na/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi sa le sbram 'byung
13a4('bum): ba de lta bu ni nyung ngo / / rab 'byor de bzhin du 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bslab pa 'di la slob pa'i sems can de lta bu'ang nyung ste/ sems can gang nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs
13a5('bum): rgyas kyi sa la gnas par 'gyur ba de lta bu ni de bas ches mang ngo / / rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper na sems can gang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ba'i las yang dag par blangs te gnas pa de lta
13a6('bum): bu ni nyung ste/ sems can gang khams kyi rgyal phran du 'gyur ba'i las yang dag par blangs shing gnas pa de lta bu ni ches mang ngo // rab 'byor de bzhin du sems can gang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i
13a7('bum): lam 'dir 'jug pa de lta bu'ang nyung ste/ sems can gang nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sa la gnas par 'gyur ba de lta bu ni de bas ches mang ngo // rab 'byor gang yang byang chub sems
13b1('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs pa de dag pas ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang de bzhin nyid du nan tan byed pa de lta
13b2('bum): bu ches nyung ngo / / de bas kyang sems can gang nyan thos sam/ rang sangs rgyas su gnas par 'gyur ba de lta bu ni ches mang ngo // rab 'byor gang yang byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i rigs
13b3('bum): kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la spyod cing the tsom med par phyir mi ldog pa'i sa gnon pa de dag pas ni/ gang phyir ldog pa'i sa gnon par 'gyur ba de lta bu ni
13b4('bum): ches mang ngo / / rab 'byor de bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpo' chen po phyir mi ldog pa'i sa 'thob par 'dod pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sar chud par 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol
13b5('bum): tu phyin pa zab mo 'di nyid la bslab par bya'o/ / rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ ser sna dang ldan pa'i sems mi
13b6('bum): skye'o/ / tshul khrims ngan pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// 'khrug pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// le lo dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// g.yong ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// shes
13b7('bum): rab 'chal pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / 'dod chags dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// zhe sdang dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// gti mug dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// tha ba dang ldan pa'i
14a1('bum): sems mi skye'o/ / gzugs dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// 'du shes dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// 'du byed dang ldan pa'i sems
14a2('bum): mi skye'o/ / rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mig dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rna ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sna dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lce dang ldan pa'i sems
14a3('bum): mi skye'o/ / lus dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// yid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// gzugs dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sgra dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// dri dang ldan pa'i sem mi skye'o// /
14a4('bum): ro dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// reg dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// chos dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mig gi rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa
14a5('bum): dang ldan pa'i sems mi skyo'o/ / sna'i rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lce'i rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lus kyi rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o//
14a6('bum): yid kyi rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mig gi 'dus te reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sna'i 'dus te reg po dang
14a7('bum): ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / lce'i 'dus te reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// /
14b1('bum): mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba
14b2('bum): dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// yid kyi
14b3('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / sa'i khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// chu'i khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// me'i khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi
14b4('bum): skye'o/ / rlung gi khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// nam mkha'i khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rnam par shes pa'i khams dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// ma rig pa dang
14b5('bum): ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / 'du byed dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// ming dang gzugs dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// skye mched drug
14b6('bum): dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / reg pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// tshor ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sred pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// len pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi
14b7('bum): skye'o/ / srid pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// skye ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rga shi dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// tshul
15a1('bum): khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang

15a3('bum): mi skye'o/ / phyi stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// phyi nang stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// chen po stong pa nyid dang ldan

15a6('bum): nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / chos thams cad stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid dang ldan
15a7('bum): ba'i sems mi skye'o/ / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems
15b1('bum): mi skye'o/ / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// yang dag par spong ba dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// dbang
15b2('bum): po dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / stobs dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// byang chub kyi yan lag dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa dang ldan pa'i sems
15b3('bum): mi skye'o/ / 'phags pa'i bden pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// bsam gtan dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// gzugs med pa'i snyoms/
15b4('bum): par 'jug pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rnam par thar pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rnam par thar
15b5('bum): pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// ting nge 'dzin dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o//

15b7('bum): pa'i sems mi skye'o/ / snying rje chen po dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dris pa dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang ldan pa'i sem
16a1('bum): mi skye'o/ / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// dgra bcom pa nyid dang ldan pa'i
16a2('bum): sems mi skye'o/ / rang byang chub dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i sems mi skye'o//
16a3('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab 'byor 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos gang yang dmigs pa med de/ ma dmigs pas chos gang
16a4('bum): la'ang sems bskyed pa med do/ / rab 'byor de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad yongs su zin
16a5('bum): pabar 'gyur ro/ / pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad 'dus par 'gyur ro// pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad dang 'thun par spyad par 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab 'byor de ni 'di ltar shes rab
16a6('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'dir pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad 'dus so/ / rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper na 'jig tshogs su lta bar lta ba'i rnam pa drug cu rtsa gnyis po thams cad kyang 'dus pa yin te/
16a7('bum): rab 'byor de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'dir pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad 'dus so// rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper na skyes bu dus byas par gyur pa'i 'tsho ba'i dbang po 'gags pas dbang
16b1('bum): bopo thams cad 'gag par 'gyur ro/ / rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la spyod pas/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad 'dus pa yin/
16b2('bum): te/ rab 'byor de bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu 'gro bar 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la bslab
16b3('bum): par bya'o/ / rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la bslob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu gyur pa la slob pa yin no//
16b4('bum): rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can gang ji snyed cig 'khod pa de dag mang ba yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das mang ngo //
16b5('bum): bde bar gshegs pa mang ngo // bcom ldan 'das ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi sems can rnams kyang mang ba lags na stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can rnams
16b6('bum): lta smos kyang ci 'tshal/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can gang ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad snga phyi med
16b7('bum): par mi'i lus thob par gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas la/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad re re la'ang sku tshe'i mthar phyin gyi
17a1('bum): bar du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos rgyun mi chad par na bzab dang / bsod snyoms dang / gzims cha dang / snyun gyi rkyen sman dang
17a2('bum): yo byad mang pos bsnyen bkur byas na/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de'i bsod nams de'i rgyus mang du 'phel lem/ gsol pa/
17a3('bum): bcom ldan 'das mang ngo // bde bar gshegs pa mang ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de bas kyang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang shes rab kyi pha
17a4('bum): rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'dzin cing 'chang ba dang / klog cing kun chub par byed pa dang / tshul bzhin du yid la byed cing de bzhin nyid du nan tan byed na/ de'i bsod nams ches mang du 'phel lo//
17a5('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni de ltar don chen por 'gyur ba ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
17a6('bum): bsgrub pa'o/ / rab 'byor de bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems can thams cad kyi bla na med par 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang / sems can mgon med pa thams cad kyi mgon du
17a7('bum): 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang / skyabs med pa rnams kyi skyabs su 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang / gnas med pa rnams kyi gnas su 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang / long ba rnams kyi mig tu 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang
17b1('bum): mun par gnas pa rnams kyi sgron mar 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas su 'gyur ba 'thob par 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul khong du chud par 'dod pa dang / rnam par rol pas rnam par rtse
17b2('bum): bar 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi seng ge'i nga ro bsgrag par 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnga brdung bar 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi dung 'bud par 'dod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi gtam bya bar
17b3('bum): 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la bslab par bya'o// rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ni//
17b4('bum): phun sum tshogs pa gang thob par bya ba de dag las mi 'thob pa gang yang med do// rab 'byor gyi gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi phun sum tshogs pa'ang des thob par bgyi ba lags
17b5('bum): sam/ rtarang sangs rgyas kyi phun sum tshogs pa'ang des thob par bgyi ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor nyan thos kyi phun sum tshogs pa'ang des 'thob
17b6('bum): par bya/ rang sangs rgyas kyi phun sum tshogs pa'ang des 'thob par bya ste/ de la gnas par mi bya/ 'dug par mi bya'i/ shes pa dang mthong bas de dag mthong bar bya ste/ 'da' bar bya//
17b7('bum): byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med par chud par bya'o// rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang nye bar gyur pa yin te/
18a1('bum): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'chang rgya'o// rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ lha dang / mi dang
18a2('bum): lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten na sbyin pa'i gnas su 'gyur ba yin te/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ de ma yin pa'i sbyin pa'i gnas nyan
18a3('bum): thos dang rang sangs rgyas gang ji snyed po de dag thams cad zil gyis gnan cing 'gro bar 'gyur ba yin/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang nye bar gyur pa yin/ rab 'byor de ltar slob pa'i
18a4('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi gtong zhing shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ma bral ba'o// /
18a5('bum): rab 'byor de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las yong su mi nyam pa'i chos can du
18a6('bum): rig par bya ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sa ring du byed cing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dang nye bar gyur pa yin/ gal te yang de 'di snyam du 'di ni shes rab kyi pha
18a7('bum): rol tu phyin pa'o/ / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'dis rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid bsgrub par bya'o snyam ste/ gal te de ltar shes na shes rab kyi pha
18b1('bum): rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do/ / gal te 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'di na yod do zhes bya bar shes pa med de/ gang gi shes rab kyi pha rol tu
18b2('bum): phyin par 'gyur ba dang / gang gis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin par 'gyur ba dang / gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas byung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
18b3('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba de ltar du'ang mi shes mi mthong zhing de 'di snyam ste/ chos kyi dbyings dang / de bzhin nyid dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' gnas pa'i phyir/ 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
18b4('bum): pa'ang ma yin/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'di na yod pa'ang ma yin/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'dis ni chos gang yang 'byung bar 'gyur ba'ang med do zhes/ rab 'byor de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub
18b5('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa yin no/ / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa las le'u bzhi bcu brgyad do// /
18b6('bum): de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin 'di snyam du sems par gyur te/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bzod pa'i
18b7('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang spyod/ nang stong pa nyid dang / phyi stong pa nyid dang /
19a1('bum): phyi nang stong pa nyid dang / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang / chen po stong pa nyid dang / don dam pa stong pa nyid dang / 'dus byas stong pa nyid dang / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid
19a2('bum): dang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dang / thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid dang / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid dang / rang bzhin stong pa nyid dang / chos thams cad stong pa nyid dang /
19a3('bum): rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dang / mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid dang / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dang / ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la'ang spyod/ dran pa nye
19a4('bum): par gzhag pa bzhi dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs lnga dang / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan
19a5('bum): lag brgyad pa la'ang spyod/ 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dang / bsam gtan bzhi dang / tshad med pa bzhi dang / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la'ang spyod/ rnam par thar pa brgyad
19a6('bum): dang / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa dang / mngon par shes pa rnams la'ang spyod/
19a7('bum): ting nge 'dzin rnams dang / gzungs kyi sgo rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / snying
19b1('bum): rje chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la'ang spyod bzhin du/ sems can thams cad zil gyis gnon na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
19b2('bum): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par gyur na lta ci smos/ sems can gang gi sems rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'jug pa de dag kyang thob pa legs par thob cing / de dag gi 'tsho ba
19b3('bum): legs par 'tsho ba yin na/ gang gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dag lta ci smos/ sems can gang gis yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems
19b4('bum): bskyed de/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di nyan pa de dag ni kun gyis yid du 'ong bar bya ba yin no snyam nas/ de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis me tog man dar ba mang po blangs te/ bcom ldan
19b5('bum): 'das gang na ba der song nas/ me tog man da ra ba de dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la gtor to// mngon par gtor to// rab tu
19b6('bum): gtor to/ / de ltar gtor te mngon par gtor ba dang // rab tu gtor ba byas nas tshig 'di skad ces brjod do// dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis gang zag byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa gang
19b7('bum): gis/ / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu dmigs pa de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi chos
20a1('bum): rnams yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ rang byung gi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ zag pa med pa'i chos rnams yong su rdzogs par gyur cig/ bcom
20a2('bum): l dan 'das bdag ni gang zag byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs pa slar ldog par 'gyur bar sems 'ga' tsam yang skye ba ma
20a3('bum): mchis so/ / bcom ldan 'das bdag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po slar log ste/ nyan thos sam rang sangs rgyas su 'gyur bar sems 'ga' tsam yang skye ba ma mchis kyi/ zla
20a4('bum): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mos pa skyed cing / yang dang yang du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam 'debs pa dang / 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal mang po 'di
20a5('bum): dag mthong nas/ lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi don du mos/ sman par mos/ bde bar mos shing legs par bgyi bar mos te/ sems bskyed pa de lta bu
20a6('bum): ngag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni 'di ltar rtog ste/ ci bdag brgal nas sems can ma brgal ba sgrol bar 'gyur ram/ ci bdag grol nas sems can ma grol
20a7('bum): ba 'grol bar 'gyur ram/ ci bdag dbugs phyin nas sems can dbugs ma phyung ba dbugs 'byin par 'gyur ram/ ci bdag yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas sems can yongs su mya ngan
20b1('bum): las ma 'das pa yongs su mya ngan las zlo bar 'gyur ram zhes rtog par bgyid de/ bcom ldan 'das de ltar theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi
20b2('bum): sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar bgyid pa dang / yun ring po nas spyod spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang
20b3('bum): bar bgyid pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar bgyid pa dang / skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i byang
20b4('bum): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar bgyid na/ rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo de'i bsod nams ji tsam zhig 'phel bar
20b5('bum): 'gyur/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// koT shI ka gling chen po bzhi pa'i 'jig
20b6('bum): rten gyi khams ni skra'i rtse mo'i tshad kyis tshad gzung bar rung yang srid kyi/ de dag gi rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa'i bsod nams la ni tshad med do// ko 'u shi ka stong
20b7('bum): gi 'jig rten gyi khams ni kwa'i rtse mo'i tshad kyis tshad gzung bar rung yang srid kyi/ de dag gi rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa'i bsod nams la ni tshad med do// ko'u shi ka stong
21a1('bum): gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ni skra'i rtse mo'i tshad kyis tshang gzung bar rung yang srid kyi/ de dag gi rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa'i bsod nams
21a2('bum): ni tshad med do/ / ko'u shi ka stong gsum gyi stong chen popo 'jig rten gyi khams ni skra'i rtse mo'i tshad kyis tshad gzung bar rung yang srid kyi/ de dag gi rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed
21a3('bum): pa'i bsod nams la ni tshad med do/ / ko'u shi ka stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgya mtsho chen po rnams la chu'i phung po ji snyed cig yod pa de ni/ skra'i rtse mo brgyar gsha
21a4('bum): pa'i cha gcig gis chu'i thigs pa blangs pa'i tshad kyis tshad gzung bar rung yang srid kyi/ de dag gi rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa'i bsod nams la ni tshad med do// de skad ces
21a5('bum): bka' stsal pa dang / lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gang sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar mi bgyid pa'i sems can
21a6('bum): de dag ni bdud kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ / bcom ldan 'das gang sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar mi bgyid pa'i sems can de dag ni bdud kyi phyogs su gyur pa'o// bcom ldan 'das
21a7('bum): gang sems bskyed pa de dgal rjes su yi rang bar mi bgyid pa'i sems can de dag ni bdud kyi gnas nas shi 'phos pa'o/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das gang gis sems bskyed pa 'di bsgrubs
21b1('bum): te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo ba'i sems can de dag ni bdud kyi gnas 'jig par bgyid pa ste/ gang bla na med pa yang dag pa rdzogs par byang chub tu
21b2('bum): sems bskyed pa'i sems de dag ni rjes su yi rang bar bgyi ba ste/ gang gis sangs rgyas yongs su ma btang ba dang / chos yongs su ma btang ba dang / dge 'dun yongs su ma btang ba de dag
21b3('bum): gis sems bskyed pa de dag la rjes su yi rang bar bgyi'o/ / rjes su yi rang nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngo bar bgyi ste/ ji ltar gnyis kyi 'du shes su mi 'gyur ba
21b4('bum): dang gnyis su ma mchis pa'i 'du shes su'ang mi 'gyur ba de ltar yongs su bsngo bar bgyi'o/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ ko'u shi ka de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad
21b5('bum): smras pa de bzhin no/ / ko'u shi ka gang sems bskyed pa 'di dag la rjes su yi rang bar byed pa de dag ni myur du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams
21b6('bum): mnyes par byed par 'gyur te/ mnyes par byas nas kyang thugs byung bar mi 'gyur ro// de de ltar rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag dang ldan pa dag ni gang
21b7('bum): dang gang du skyed pa de dang de dag tu rim gror bya bar 'gyur ro/ / bkur stir bya bar 'gyur ro// phu dud du bya bar 'gyur ro// mchod par bya bar 'gyur ro// des nam yang gzugs yid du mi
22a1('bum): 'ong ba mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ / nam yang sgra yid du mi 'ong ba thos par mi 'gyur ro// nam yang dri yid du mi 'ong ba tshor bar mi 'gyur ro// nam yang ro yid du mi 'ong ba
22a2('bum): myong bar mi 'gyur ro/ / nam yang reg yid du mi 'ong ba reg par mi 'gyur ro// nam yang chos yid du mi 'ong ba shes par mi 'gyur ro// nam yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
22a3('bum): dang 'bral bar mi 'gyur te/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro zhing / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la bsnyen bkur byed pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba skyed par 'gyur ro// de
22a4('bum): ci'i phyir zhe na/ ko'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar rigs kyi bu dang rigs kyi bu mo de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa dang / spyod pa la zhugs pa
22a5('bum): dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / skye ba gcig gis thogs pa tshad med grangs med dpag tu med pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag la rjes su yi rang bar byas pa'i phyir te/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de
22a6('bum): ngag gis rnam par 'phel bas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nye bar gyur pa yin te/ de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas
22a7('bum): nas/ sems can tshad med grangs med dpag tu med pa yongs su mya ngan las zlo bar 'gyur ro// ko'u shi ka rnam grangs des kyang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo des ci nas kyang sems
22b1('bum): med pa dang / sems ma yin pa gzhan yang med par theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba la rjes su yi rang bar byas shing /
22b2('bum): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bar bya'o// sems med pa dang / sems ma yin pa gzhan yang med par spyad pa spyod pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / skye ba
22b3('bum): gcig gis thogs pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag la'ang rjes su yi rang bar byas shing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bar bya'o// /
22b4('bum): / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa bam po nyis brgya zhe brgyad pa// / de nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//
22b5('bum): bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na sgyu ma lta bu'i sems/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
22b6('bum): stsal pa/ rta rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ sgyu ma lta bu'i sems de khyod kyis yang dag par rjes su mthong ngam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags te/ bcom ldan 'das
22b7('bum): bdag gis sgyu ma yang dag par rjes su ma mthong / sgyu mo lta bu'i sems de'ang yang dag par rjes su ma mthong ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/
23a1('bum): de de ltar sgyu ma'ang ma mthong / sgyu ma lta bu'i sems kyang ma mthong na/ sems gang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par
23a2('bum): 'tshang rgya ba'i sems de khyod kyis yang dag par rjes su mthong ngam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam
23a3('bum): du sems/ sgyu ma dang sgyu ma lta bu'i sems de las gud na chos gang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i chos de khyod kyis yang dag par rjes su
23a4('bum): mthong ngam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags te/ bcom ldan 'das sgyu ma dang sgyu ma lta bu'i sems las gud na chos gang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu
23a5('bum): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba de bdag gis yang dag par rjes su ma mthong ngo / / bcom ldan 'das de ltar bdag gis chos gzhan yang dag par rjes su ma mthong na/ mchis pa
23a6('bum): 'am ma mchis pa'i chos gang zhig bdag gis bstan par bgyi/ chos gang shin tu dben pa de ni mchis pa'am ma mchis par mi 'gyur ro// chos gang shin tu dben pa de ni bla na med pa
23a7('bum): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgya ste/ ma mchis pa'i chos kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi
23b1('bum): rgya'o/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar gang nyon mongs par 'gyur ba 'am/ rnam par byang bar 'gyur ba'i chos thams cad ni ma mchis shing yongs su ma
23b2('bum): mchis pa'o/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o//
23b3('bum): brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol
23b4('bum): tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / nang stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// phyi stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// phyi nang stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni shin
23b5('bum): tu dben pa'o/ / chen po stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// don dam pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni shin tu dngabe na pa'o// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni shin tu
23b6('bum): dben pa'o/ / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rang bzhin
23b7('bum): stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o//
24a1('bum): dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o//
24a2('bum): dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// yang dag par spong ba rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// dbang po rnams ni shin tu
24a3('bum): bden pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / bsam gtan rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// tshad med pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni /
24a4('bum): shin tu dben pa'o// rnam pa thar pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang /
24a5('bum): mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// ting nge 'dzin rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// gzungs kyi sgo rnams ni//
24a6('bum): shin tu dben pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ni shin tu dben pa'o// mi 'jigs pa bzhi ni shin tu dben pa'o// so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni shin tu dben pa'o//
24b1('bum): byams pa chen po ni shin tu dben pa'o// snying rje chen po ni shin tu dben pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ni shin tu dben pa'o// rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu ni
24b2('bum): shin tu dben pa'o/ / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni shin tu dben pa'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni shin tu dben pa'o// dgra bcom pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rang byang chub
24b3('bum): ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// chos gang shin tu dben pa de ni bsgom par bgyi ba'ang
24b4('bum): ma lags/ rnam par bsgom par bgyi ba'ang ma lags te/ de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'i slad du chos gang yang bsgrub pa ma mchis so// shes rab kyi pha rol tu
24b5('bum): phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa lags na/ ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rten cing / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bla ni med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
24b6('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang shin tu dben pa lags na/ de ji ltar dben pas dben pa 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur//
24b7('bum): / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor legs so legs so// rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa/
25a1('bum): bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben
25a2('bum): pa'o/ / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// nang stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// phyi stong pa nyid ni
25a3('bum): tu dben pa'o/ / phyi nang stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// chen po stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// don dam pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben
25a4('bum): pa'o/ / 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// thog ma dang tha ma med
25a5('bum): pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o//
25a6('bum): rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid na shin tu dben pa'o// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni
25a7('bum): tu dben pa'o/ / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// yang dag par spong ba rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o//
25b1('bum): rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// dbang po rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// stobs rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o//
25b2('bum): 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// bsam gtan rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o// tshad med pa rnams ni

25b4('bum): pa rnams ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni shin tu dben pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams ni shin tu dben

25b6('bum): tu dben pa'o/ / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni shin tu dben pa'o// byams pa chen po ni shin tu dben pa'o// snying rje chen po ni shin tu dben pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres
25b7('bum): pa bco brgyad ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu ni shin tu dben pa'o// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni shin tu dben pa'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni shin tu dben/
26a1('bum): pa'o// dgra bcom pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rang byang chub ni shin tu dben pa'o// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid ni shin tu dben pa'o// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
26a2('bum): ni shin tu dben pa'o/ / rab 'byor ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
26a3('bum): shin tu dben pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / nang stong pa
26a4('bum): nyid nga shin tu dben pa dang / phyi stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / phyi nang stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / chen po stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang
26a5('bum): don dam pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / 'dus byas stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben
26a6('bum): pa dang / thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / rang bzhin stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / chos thams cad stong pa
26a7('bum): nyid shin tu dben pa dang / rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / za/
26b1('bum): stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / yang dag par spong ba rnams shin tu dben pa
26b2('bum): dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / dbang po rnams shin tu dben pa dang / stobs rnams shin tu dben pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams shin tu dben pa dang
26b3('bum): 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa shin tu dben pa dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / bsam gtan rnams shin tu dben pa dang / tshad med pa rnams shin tu
26b4('bum): dben pa dang / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / rnam par thar pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams
26b5('bum): shin tu dben pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa shin tu dben pa dang / mngon par shes pa bzhing shin tu dben pa dang / ting nge 'dzin
26b6('bum): rnams shin tu dben pa dang / gzungs kyi sgo rnams shin tu dben pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu shin tu dben pa dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi shin tu dben pa dang / so so/

27a1('bum): pa dang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu shin tu dben pa dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu shin tu dben pa dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu shin tu dben/
27a2('bum): pa dang dgra bcom pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / rang byang chub shin tu dben pa dang / lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin

27a4('bum): pa shin tu dben pa ma gyur/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben par ma gyur/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben par ma gyur/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa

28a6('bum): lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid shin tu dben par ma gyur/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin tu dben par ma gyur na// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin par mi 'gyur ro//

29a1('bum): ro/ de tshad med pa rnams su mi 'gyur ro// de gzugs med pa'i snyom par 'jug pa rnams su mi 'gyur ro// de rnam par thar pa rnams su mi

29a6('bum): 'gyur ro/ / de dgra bcom pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro// de rang byang chub tu mi 'gyur ro// de lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro// de rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro//
29a7('bum): rab 'byor de bas na ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
29b1('bum): shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa shin
29b2('bum): tu dben pa dang / ji ltar nang stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar phyi stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar phyi nang stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar stong ba nyid stong pa nyid shin tu
29b3('bum): dben pa dang / ji ltar chen po stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar don dam pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar 'dus byas stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar 'dus ma
29b4('bum): byas stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dor ba med pa
29b5('bum): stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rang bzhin stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar chos thams cad stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa
29b6('bum): dang ji ltar mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dngos po med pa stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dngos po
29b7('bum): med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar yang dag par spong ba rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rtswa
30a1('bum): 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dbang po rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar stobs rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar byang chub kyi yan lag
30a2('bum): rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar bsam
30a3('bum): gtan rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar tshad med pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rnam par
30a4('bum): thar pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma
30a5('bum): med pa dang / smon pa med pa shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar mngon par shes pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar ting nge 'dzin rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar gzungs kyi
30a6('bum): sgo rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar mi 'jigs pa rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar so so yang dag par rig pa
30a7('bum): rnams shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar byams pa chen po shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar snying rje chen po shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad shin tu dben pa dang
30b1('bum): ji ltar rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar dgra bcom
30b2('bum): pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rang byang chub shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid shin tu dben pa dang / ji ltar rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin tu dben pa de ltar
30b3('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma brten par yang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgya/ dben pas dben pa mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
30b4('bum): mi rgyu ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgyu bas na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma brten par mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang ma
30b5('bum): rgyu'o/ / gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni don zab mo la spyod pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor
30b6('bum): de bzhin no/ / de de bzhin te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni don zab mo la spyod pa'o// rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de ltar don zab
30b7('bum): mo la spyod cing / 'di lta ste/ nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar 'gyur ba'i don de mngon du mi byed pa ni de dka' ba byed pa'o// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
31a1('bum): gsungs pa'i don bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na/ dka' ba cung zad kyang mi bgyid na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dka' ba bgyid pa lags/
31a2('bum): de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar gang mngon du bgyi ba'i don de'ang mi dmigs/ gang gis mngon du bgyi ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa de'ang mi dmigs//
31a3('bum): gang mngon du bgyi ba'i chos de'ang mi dmigs te/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad gang mngon du bgyis pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par
31a4('bum): batshang rgya bar 'gyur ba'i don mngon du bgyi ba de lta bu'ang gang zhig mchis/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang gang zhig gis mngon du bgyi/ chos mngon du bgyi ba de lta bu'ang gang zhig
31a5('bum): mchis rta bcom ldan 'das 'di ni mi dmigs pa'i spyod pa ste/ de la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni chos thams cad la mun pa ma mchis pa 'thob bo//
31a6('bum): bcom ldan 'das gal te de skad du bstan pa la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i sems mi 'dzum yongs su mi 'dzum zhing / mi 'jigs mi sdang skrag par mi 'gyur na/
31a7('bum): bcom ldan 'das de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa ste/ de ni spyod do zhes bgyi bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong
31b1('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o zhes bgyi bar yang dag
31b2('bum): par rjes su mi mthong ngo / / bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa de ni/ 'di snam du bdag gis nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas
31b3('bum): kyis ni rgyad bsring bar bya ste/ bdag ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du nye bar gyur to snyam yang mi bgyid do/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni 'di ltar bdag ni
31b4('bum): la la dang ni ring ngo / / la la dang ni nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na// bcom ldan 'das nam mkha' la bye brag ma mchis shing mi g.yo ba dang / rnam par
31b5('bum): rtog pa ma mchis pa'i slad du ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'ang / 'di ltar bdag las nyan thos
31b6('bum): sam rang sangs rgyas kyi sa ni ring gi/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sa ni nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha
31b7('bum): rol tu phyin pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na sgyu ma'i skyes bu ni 'di ltar bdag las sgyu ma ni ring ngo // sgyu ma'i mkhan po ni nye'o//
32a1('bum): skye bo'i tshogs 'di ltar 'dus pa ni bdag las ring ngo zhe bam/ nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das sgyu ma'i skyes
32a2('bum): bu ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la skrod pa'ang / 'di ltar bdag las nyan
32a3('bum): thos sam rang sangs rgyas kyis ni ring ngo / / bla na med pa yang dag por rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha
32a4('bum): rol tu phyin pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste// dper na gzugs brnyan ni 'di ltar bdag las dmigs pa gang gi gzugs brnyan 'byung ba de ni nye//
32a5('bum): gang me long dang snod chus gang ba'i nang du byung ba de ni bdag las ring ngo zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das gzugs brnyan rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du ste/
32a6('bum): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'ang / 'di ltar bdag las nyan thos sam rang sangs rgyas kyi sa ni ring ngo /
32a7('bum): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe no// bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du
32b1('bum): bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ni sdug pa dang mi sdug pa ma mchis so/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang gis 'di la sdug pa 'am/ mi sdug par 'gyur ba'i ngo bo
32b2('bum): nyid mi dmigs pa'i slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la ni sdug pa'am/ mi sdug par 'gyur ba
32b3('bum): gang yang ma mchis so/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang sdug pa'am/ mi sdug par 'gyur bar gang yang ma mchis so// bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/
32b4('bum): dper na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni rnam par rtog pa thams cad spangs pa'o// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'
32b5('bum): sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'ang / rnam par rtog pa thams cad spangs pa ste// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
32b6('bum): pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i spyad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa ni// 'di ltar nga las nyan thos sam rang sangs rgyas kyis ni ring ngo //
32b7('bum): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni zhi'o zhes bgyi bar mi dgongs so// de ci'i slad du de ni/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra
33a1('bum): pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'ang / 'di ltar bdag
33a2('bum): las nyan thos kyi sa 'am rang sangs rgyas kyi sa ni ring ngo / / bla na med pa la dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni nye'o zhes bgyi bar mi sems so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das
33a3('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na de bzhin gshegs pas sprul pazhi basprul pa mdza na/ de ni don gang gi slad du sprul pa de'i
33a4('bum): don sbyor te/ sprul pa ni mi rtog rnam par mi rtog go// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang don gang gi slad du brjod pa'i don de'ang bgyid de/ shes rab kyi pha
33a5('bum): rol tu phyin pa de ni mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na shing mkhan nam/ shing mkhan gyi slob ma mkhas pa zhig gis bud med kyi gzugs sam/
33a6('bum): skyes pa'i gzugs sam/ glang po'i gzugs sam/ chibs rta'i gzugs sam/ glang gi gzugs kyi 'khrul 'khor zhig sbyar na/ de don gang gi slad du bgyis pa'i don de sgrub kyang
33a7('bum): 'khrul 'khor de ni rnam par mi rtog go/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang don gang gi slad du brjod pa'i don de bgyid kyang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa de ni rnam
33b1('bum): par mi rtog pa'o/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus/ tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
33b2('bum): pa 'ba' zhig rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'on te bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'on te brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog
33b3('bum): pa yin nam/ 'on te bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'on te tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'on te sbyin pa'i
33b4('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ / rab 'byor gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa'o// brtson
33b5('bum): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa'o/ / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog
33b6('bum): pa'i/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa'o// smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor ci gzugs kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ tshor ba'ang
33b7('bum): rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'du shes kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'du byed kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin
34a1('bum): nam/ mig kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rna ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ snabang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lce'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/
34a2('bum): lus kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ yid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ gzugs kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sgrubang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ dri'ang rnam par mi rtog
34a3('bum): pa yin nam/ ro'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ reg kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ chos kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mig gi rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa
34a4('bum): namama'i rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sna'i rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lce'i rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lus
34a5('bum): kyi rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rna ba'i
34a6('bum): 'dus te reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lus kyi 'dus te/
34a7('bum): reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor babang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rna ba'i
34b1('bum): / 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor sang rnam par mi rtog pa yin na//
34b2('bum): lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sa'i khams kyang rnam par mi
34b3('bum): rtog pa yin nam/ chu'i khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ me'i khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rlung gi khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ nam mkha'i khams kyang
34b4('bum): rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rnam par shes pa'i khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ ma rig pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'du byed kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam//
34b5('bum): rnam par shes pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ ming dang gzugs kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ skye mched drug kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ reg pa'ang rnam par mi
34b6('bum): rtog pa yin nam/ tshor ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sred pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ len pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ srid pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa
34b7('bum): yin nam/ skye ba'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rga shi'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ tshul khrims kyi pha
35a1('bum): rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa
35a2('bum): yin nam/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ nang stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam
35a3('bum): phyi stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ chen po stong pa nyid kyang rnam
35a4('bum): par mi rtog pa yin nam/ don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyang rnam par
35a5('bum): mi rtog pa yin nam/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid
35a6('bum): kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa
35a7('bum): nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ ngo bo nyid stong
35b1('bum): pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/
35b2('bum): yang dag par spong ba rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ dbang po rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ stobs
35b3('bum): rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam
35b4('bum): 'phag pa'i bden pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ bsam gtan rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ tshad med pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam
35b5('bum): gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rnam par thar pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa
35b6('bum): rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mngon par shes pa
35b7('bum): rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
36a1('bum): stobs rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ mi 'jigs pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam//
36a2('bum): byams pa chen po'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ snying rje chen po'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rgyun du
36a3('bum): zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lan cig phyir bong ba'i 'bras bu'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'ang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/
36a4('bum): dgra bcom pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rang byang chub kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ rnam pa thams
36a5('bum): cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'dus byas kyi khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/ 'dus ma byas kyi khams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa yin nam/
36a6('bum): rab 'byor gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu chos thams cad ni rnam par mi rtog pa'o// smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gal te de ltar chos thams cad
36a7('bum): rnam par mi rtog pa yin na/ sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten dang / lha dang / mi'i 'gro ba lngar 'khor ba zhes tha dad du dbye ba ci las
36b1('bum): 'ongs rta rgyun du zhugs pa dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba dang / phyir mi bong ba dang / dgra bcom pa dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / sangs rgyas bcom
36b2('bum): ldan 'das su brjod pa'ang ci las gyur/ rab 'byor gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu sems can gang phyin ci log las byung ba'i las lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyis
36b3('bum): mngon par 'du byed pa de dag 'di lta bu'i skye mched mngon par sgrub ste/ las kyi rnam par smin pa phung po'i gzhi can rnams rnam par rtog pa las byung ba yongs su bzung zhing / sems
36b4('bum): can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten dang / lha dang / mi'i 'gro ba mngon par sgrub po// tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu gang khyod kyis 'di skad du/
36b5('bum): rgyun du zhugs par brjod pa ci las gyur/ lan cig phyir 'ong bar brjod pa ci las gyur/ phyir mi 'ong bar brjod pa ci las gyur/ dgra bcom par brjod pa ci las gyur/ rang sangs rgyas
36b6('bum): su brjod pa ci las gyur/ byang chub sems dpar brjod pa ci las gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su brjod pa ci las gyur ces zer ba ni// tshed
36b7('bum): ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu rnam par mi rtog pa las rgyun du zhugs par brjod do/ / rnam par mi rtog pa las rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bur brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las lan cig phyir
37a1('bum): 'ong bar brjod do/ / rnam par mi rtog pa las lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bur brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las phyir mi 'ong bar brjod do// rnam par mi rtog
37a2('bum): pa las phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bur brjod do/ / rnam par mi rtog pa las dgra bcom par brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las dgra bcom pa nyid du brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las rang
37a3('bum): sangs rgyas su brjod do/ / rnam par mi rtog pa las rang byang chub tu brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las sangs rgyas su brjod do// rnam par mi rtog pa las byang chub tu brjod do// tshe dang
37a4('bum): l dan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'das pa'i dus na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang ji snyed cig byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag kyang rnam par rtog pa mi

37b1('bum): ldan 'das de dag kyang rnam par rtog pa mi mnga' zhing / rnam par rtog pa spangs pa sha stag go/ de ltar tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu rnam grangs des na/ chos thams cad rnam par rtog pa med

39a1('bum): de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas ni snying po med pa nyid kyang mi dmigs shing yang dag par rjes
